allows dynamic extension of the API server's admission control. Here's the comprehensive trace across the codebase:\\n\\n### 1. Generic Webhook Dispatcher (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/)\\n\\nThe foundation of the webhook system is defined in `generic/interfaces.go` which establishes the core abstractions:\\n- **`Dispatcher` interface**: The primary interface that handles dispatching admission requests to webhooks. It has a `Dispatch()` method that processes webhooks and returns errors if validation fails.\\n- **`Source` interface**: Provides a list of webhooks to be called via `Webhooks()` method and tracks synchronization status with `HasSynced()`.\\n- **`WebhookInvocation` struct**: Represents a specific webhook to be called with its associated resource, subresource, and kind information.\\n- **`VersionedAttributeAccessor` interface**: Provides access to versioned attributes for different API versions of the admission request.\\n\\nThe `generic/webhook.go` file implements the generic `Webhook` struct which contains the shared logic for admission processing. The `NewWebhook()` factory function creates webhook instances with proper initialization of client managers, matchers, and dispatcher factories. The `ShouldCallHook()` method determines whether a specific webhook should be invoked based on matching rules, namespace selectors, object selectors, and match conditions.\\n\\n### 2. WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go)\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a unified abstraction over both mutating and validating webhooks. It abstracts the differences between:\\n- **`MutatingWebhook`** and **`ValidatingWebhook`** types from the API\\n\\nThe interface provides:\\n- `GetName()`, `GetUID()`, `GetConfigurationName()`: Webhook identification\\n- `GetClientConfig()`, `GetRules()`, `GetFailurePolicy()`, `GetMatchPolicy()`: Webhook configuration access\\n- `GetNamespaceSelector()`, `GetObjectSelector()`: Selector access\\n- `GetAdmissionReviewVersions()`, `GetTimeoutSeconds()`, `GetSideEffects()`: Webhook behavior control\\n- `GetCompiledMatcher()`: Access to CEL-compiled match conditions\\n- `GetMutatingWebhook()`, `GetValidatingWebhook()`: Type-specific accessors\\n\\nTwo concrete implementations are provided:\\n1. **`mutatingWebhookAccessor`**: Wraps a `v1.MutatingWebhook` with caching for selectors and compiled matchers\\n2. **`validatingWebhookAccessor`**: Wraps a `v1.ValidatingWebhook` with similar caching mechanisms\\n\\nFactory functions `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` create these instances with unique UIDs and configuration names.\\n\\n### 3. Configuration Managers (pkg/admission/configuration/)\\n\\nConfiguration managers handle dynamic loading and caching of webhook configurations:\\n\\n**mutating_webhook_manager.go**:\\n- `mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements the `generic.Source` interface\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates a manager that watches `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` resources\\n- Uses lazy evaluation to fetch webhook accessors from the lister\\n- Caches webhook accessors to avoid expensive CEL recompilation\\n- Calls `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` for each webhook in the configuration\\n\\n**validating_webhook_manager.go**:\\n- `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements the `generic.Source` interface  \\n- `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates a manager that watches `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` resources\\n- Similar caching and lazy evaluation as the mutating version\\n- Calls `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` for each webhook in the configuration\\n\\n### 4. Mutating Webhook Dispatcher (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go)\\n\\nThe mutating webhook dispatcher implements request mutation with **reinvocation logic**:\\n\\n**Key Features**:\\n- `mutatingDispatcher` struct implements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- `Dispatch()` method handles serial invocation of mutating webhooks\\n- **Reinvocation support**: Tracks previously invoked webhooks using `webhookReinvokeContext`\\n- **Object change detection**: Compares object state before and after webhook invocation to determine if reinvocation is needed\\n- Uses `versionedAttributeAccessor` to manage object versioning for each webhook call\\n- Applies JSON patches from webhooks to mutate the original object\\n- Handles webhook failures with configurable failure policies\\n- Records audit annotations for mutations and patch information\\n\\nThe reinvocation chain allows in-tree admission controllers to run again when webhooks modify objects, ensuring all validation rules are re-applied.\\n\\n### 5. Validating Webhook Dispatcher (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go)\\n\\nThe validating webhook dispatcher implements validation with **parallel dispatch**:\\n\\n**Key Features**:\\n- `validatingDispatcher` struct implements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- `Dispatch()` method collects all relevant webhooks, then executes them in parallel using goroutines\\n- **Parallel execution**: Uses `sync.WaitGroup` to coordinate multiple goroutine-based webhook calls\\n- Pre-caches versioned attributes to avoid recomputation during parallel execution\\n- Each webhook runs in its own goroutine with isolated error channels\\n- Proper panic recovery with `defer utilruntime.HandleCrash()`\\n- Aggregates errors from all webhooks before returning\\n- Respects request context timeouts\\n- Records validation metrics and audit annotations\\n\\nThe parallel dispatch is more efficient than serial execution since validating webhooks don't mutate objects.\\n\\n### 6. Plugin Implementations (mutating/plugin.go, validating/plugin.go)\\n\\n**Mutating Plugin**:\\n- Extends the generic `Webhook` with the `newMutatingDispatcher()` factory\\n- Provides the `newMutatingDispatcher()` function that creates `mutatingDispatcher` instances\\n\\n**Validating Plugin**:\\n- Extends the generic `Webhook` with the `newValidatingDispatcher()` factory\\n- Provides the `newValidatingDispatcher()` function that creates `validatingDispatcher` instances\\n\\n### 7. Request Handling (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go)\\n\\nHandles conversion of admission requests to AdmissionReview format:\\n- Creates `AdmissionReview` objects from admission attributes\\n- Handles version negotiation between API server and webhooks\\n- Manages response parsing and status extraction\\n\\n### 8. Matching and Predicates (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/)\\n\\nMultiple matching stages filter which webhooks should be called:\\n\\n**rules/rules.go**:\\n- `Matcher` evaluates if a request matches webhook rules\\n- Checks API group, version, resource, operation, and scope\\n- Supports wildcard matching\\n\\n**namespace/matcher.go**:\\n- `Matcher` evaluates namespace selectors\\n- Fetches namespace labels from the cluster lister\\n- Applies label selector matching\\n\\n**object/matcher.go**:\\n- `Matcher` evaluates object selectors\\n- Checks labels on both old and new objects\\n- Used for fine-grained filtering\\n\\n**matchconditions/matcher.go**:\\n- CEL-based match condition evaluation\\n- Compiles and executes CEL expressions\\n- Supports access to admission request and authorizer context\\n- Handles failure policies for evaluation errors\\n\\n### 9. API Type Definitions (kubernetes-api)\\n\\n**admissionregistration/v1/types.go**:\\n- **`MutatingWebhookConfiguration`**: Top-level resource containing a list of `MutatingWebhook` objects\\n- **`MutatingWebhook`**: Individual webhook configuration with name, client config, rules, failure policy, match policy, namespace/object selectors, side effects, timeout, admission review versions, and match conditions\\n- **`ValidatingWebhookConfiguration`**: Top-level resource containing a list of `ValidatingWebhook` objects\\n- **`ValidatingWebhook`**: Similar structure to `MutatingWebhook` but for validation-only webhooks\\n- **`MutatingWebhookConfigurationList`** and **`ValidatingWebhookConfigurationList`**: List wrappers for API operations\\n\\n**admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go**:\\n- Deprecated v1beta1 versions of the above types\\n- Maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\n### 10. Error Handling (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/)\\n\\n**statuserror.go**:\\n- `ToStatusErr()`: Converts webhook responses to Kubernetes `StatusError`\\n- `NewDryRunUnsupportedErr()`: Creates errors for webhooks not supporting dry-run\\n- Proper error message formatting with webhook names\\n\\n### Processing Flow\\n\\n1. API request arrives at the API server\\n2. Generic `Webhook` dispatcher is initialized with configuration managers as sources\\n3. `ShouldCallHook()` evaluates each webhook against the request:\\n   - Rules matching (resource, operation, API group/version)\\n   - Namespace selector matching\\n   - Object selector matching  \\n   - CEL match conditions evaluation\\n4. For mutating webhooks:\\n   - Webhooks are called serially (in configuration order, sorted by name)\\n   - Object patches are applied after each webhook\\n   - Reinvocation occurs if object changed and webhook was previously invoked\\n   - Each webhook sees the result of previous webhooks' mutations\\n5. For validating webhooks:\\n   - All matching webhooks are collected first\\n   - Webhooks are called in parallel for efficiency\\n   - Results are aggregated; any rejection fails the request\\n   - No object mutation occurs\\n6. WebhookAccessor abstraction provides uniform access to webhook configuration\\n7. Configuration managers dynamically watch and cache webhook configurations\\n8. Proper error handling and metrics recording throughout the chain\\n\\nThis architecture allows Kubernetes to support dynamic, extensible admission control while maintaining performance (parallel validating webhooks) and correctness (serial mutating with reinvocation support).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":496,"cache_read_input_tokens":91916,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":496},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5c06c150-69e8-46c3-a291-552f7f42e32a","uuid":"4dbd710d-eaef-489b-bbba-106799df8589"}

allows dynamic extension of the API server's admission control. Here's the comprehensive trace across the codebase:\\n\\n### 1. Generic Webhook Dispatcher (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/)\\n\\nThe foundation of the webhook system is defined in `generic/interfaces.go` which establishes the core abstractions:\\n- **`Dispatcher` interface**: The primary interface that handles dispatching admission requests to webhooks. It has a `Dispatch()` method that processes webhooks and returns errors if validation fails.\\n- **`Source` interface**: Provides a list of webhooks to be called via `Webhooks()` method and tracks synchronization status with `HasSynced()`.\\n- **`WebhookInvocation` struct**: Represents a specific webhook to be called with its associated resource, subresource, and kind information.\\n- **`VersionedAttributeAccessor` interface**: Provides access to versioned attributes for different API versions of the admission request.\\n\\nThe `generic/webhook.go` file implements the generic `Webhook` struct which contains the shared logic for admission processing. The `NewWebhook()` factory function creates webhook instances with proper initialization of client managers, matchers, and dispatcher factories. The `ShouldCallHook()` method determines whether a specific webhook should be invoked based on matching rules, namespace selectors, object selectors, and match conditions.\\n\\n### 2. WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go)\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a unified abstraction over both mutating and validating webhooks. It abstracts the differences between:\\n- **`MutatingWebhook`** and **`ValidatingWebhook`** types from the API\\n\\nThe interface provides:\\n- `GetName()`, `GetUID()`, `GetConfigurationName()`: Webhook identification\\n- `GetClientConfig()`, `GetRules()`, `GetFailurePolicy()`, `GetMatchPolicy()`: Webhook configuration access\\n- `GetNamespaceSelector()`, `GetObjectSelector()`: Selector access\\n- `GetAdmissionReviewVersions()`, `GetTimeoutSeconds()`, `GetSideEffects()`: Webhook behavior control\\n- `GetCompiledMatcher()`: Access to CEL-compiled match conditions\\n- `GetMutatingWebhook()`, `GetValidatingWebhook()`: Type-specific accessors\\n\\nTwo concrete implementations are provided:\\n1. **`mutatingWebhookAccessor`**: Wraps a `v1.MutatingWebhook` with caching for selectors and compiled matchers\\n2. **`validatingWebhookAccessor`**: Wraps a `v1.ValidatingWebhook` with similar caching mechanisms\\n\\nFactory functions `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` create these instances with unique UIDs and configuration names.\\n\\n### 3. Configuration Managers (pkg/admission/configuration/)\\n\\nConfiguration managers handle dynamic loading and caching of webhook configurations:\\n\\n**mutating_webhook_manager.go**:\\n- `mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements the `generic.Source` interface\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates a manager that watches `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` resources\\n- Uses lazy evaluation to fetch webhook accessors from the lister\\n- Caches webhook accessors to avoid expensive CEL recompilation\\n- Calls `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` for each webhook in the configuration\\n\\n**validating_webhook_manager.go**:\\n- `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements the `generic.Source` interface  \\n- `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates a manager that watches `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` resources\\n- Similar caching and lazy evaluation as the mutating version\\n- Calls `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` for each webhook in the configuration\\n\\n### 4. Mutating Webhook Dispatcher (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go)\\n\\nThe mutating webhook dispatcher implements request mutation with **reinvocation logic**:\\n\\n**Key Features**:\\n- `mutatingDispatcher` struct implements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- `Dispatch()` method handles serial invocation of mutating webhooks\\n- **Reinvocation support**: Tracks previously invoked webhooks using `webhookReinvokeContext`\\n- **Object change detection**: Compares object state before and after webhook invocation to determine if reinvocation is needed\\n- Uses `versionedAttributeAccessor` to manage object versioning for each webhook call\\n- Applies JSON patches from webhooks to mutate the original object\\n- Handles webhook failures with configurable failure policies\\n- Records audit annotations for mutations and patch information\\n\\nThe reinvocation chain allows in-tree admission controllers to run again when webhooks modify objects, ensuring all validation rules are re-applied.\\n\\n### 5. Validating Webhook Dispatcher (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go)\\n\\nThe validating webhook dispatcher implements validation with **parallel dispatch**:\\n\\n**Key Features**:\\n- `validatingDispatcher` struct implements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- `Dispatch()` method collects all relevant webhooks, then executes them in parallel using goroutines\\n- **Parallel execution**: Uses `sync.WaitGroup` to coordinate multiple goroutine-based webhook calls\\n- Pre-caches versioned attributes to avoid recomputation during parallel execution\\n- Each webhook runs in its own goroutine with isolated error channels\\n- Proper panic recovery with `defer utilruntime.HandleCrash()`\\n- Aggregates errors from all webhooks before returning\\n- Respects request context timeouts\\n- Records validation metrics and audit annotations\\n\\nThe parallel dispatch is more efficient than serial execution since validating webhooks don't mutate objects.\\n\\n### 6. Plugin Implementations (mutating/plugin.go, validating/plugin.go)\\n\\n**Mutating Plugin**:\\n- Extends the generic `Webhook` with the `newMutatingDispatcher()` factory\\n- Provides the `newMutatingDispatcher()` function that creates `mutatingDispatcher` instances\\n\\n**Validating Plugin**:\\n- Extends the generic `Webhook` with the `newValidatingDispatcher()` factory\\n- Provides the `newValidatingDispatcher()` function that creates `validatingDispatcher` instances\\n\\n### 7. Request Handling (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go)\\n\\nHandles conversion of admission requests to AdmissionReview format:\\n- Creates `AdmissionReview` objects from admission attributes\\n- Handles version negotiation between API server and webhooks\\n- Manages response parsing and status extraction\\n\\n### 8. Matching and Predicates (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/)\\n\\nMultiple matching stages filter which webhooks should be called:\\n\\n**rules/rules.go**:\\n- `Matcher` evaluates if a request matches webhook rules\\n- Checks API group, version, resource, operation, and scope\\n- Supports wildcard matching\\n\\n**namespace/matcher.go**:\\n- `Matcher` evaluates namespace selectors\\n- Fetches namespace labels from the cluster lister\\n- Applies label selector matching\\n\\n**object/matcher.go**:\\n- `Matcher` evaluates object selectors\\n- Checks labels on both old and new objects\\n- Used for fine-grained filtering\\n\\n**matchconditions/matcher.go**:\\n- CEL-based match condition evaluation\\n- Compiles and executes CEL expressions\\n- Supports access to admission request and authorizer context\\n- Handles failure policies for evaluation errors\\n\\n### 9. API Type Definitions (kubernetes-api)\\n\\n**admissionregistration/v1/types.go**:\\n- **`MutatingWebhookConfiguration`**: Top-level resource containing a list of `MutatingWebhook` objects\\n- **`MutatingWebhook`**: Individual webhook configuration with name, client config, rules, failure policy, match policy, namespace/object selectors, side effects, timeout, admission review versions, and match conditions\\n- **`ValidatingWebhookConfiguration`**: Top-level resource containing a list of `ValidatingWebhook` objects\\n- **`ValidatingWebhook`**: Similar structure to `MutatingWebhook` but for validation-only webhooks\\n- **`MutatingWebhookConfigurationList`** and **`ValidatingWebhookConfigurationList`**: List wrappers for API operations\\n\\n**admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go**:\\n- Deprecated v1beta1 versions of the above types\\n- Maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\n### 10. Error Handling (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/)\\n\\n**statuserror.go**:\\n- `ToStatusErr()`: Converts webhook responses to Kubernetes `StatusError`\\n- `NewDryRunUnsupportedErr()`: Creates errors for webhooks not supporting dry-run\\n- Proper error message formatting with webhook names\\n\\n### Processing Flow\\n\\n1. API request arrives at the API server\\n2. Generic `Webhook` dispatcher is initialized with configuration managers as sources\\n3. `ShouldCallHook()` evaluates each webhook against the request:\\n   - Rules matching (resource, operation, API group/version)\\n   - Namespace selector matching\\n   - Object selector matching  \\n   - CEL match conditions evaluation\\n4. For mutating webhooks:\\n   - Webhooks are called serially (in configuration order, sorted by name)\\n   - Object patches are applied after each webhook\\n   - Reinvocation occurs if object changed and webhook was previously invoked\\n   - Each webhook sees the result of previous webhooks' mutations\\n5. For validating webhooks:\\n   - All matching webhooks are collected first\\n   - Webhooks are called in parallel for efficiency\\n   - Results are aggregated; any rejection fails the request\\n   - No object mutation occurs\\n6. WebhookAccessor abstraction provides uniform access to webhook configuration\\n7. Configuration managers dynamically watch and cache webhook configurations\\n8. Proper error handling and metrics recording throughout the chain\\n\\nThis architecture allows Kubernetes to support dynamic, extensible admission control while maintaining performance (parallel validating webhooks) and correctness (serial mutating with reinvocation support).\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
